    <!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
        var path_to_root = "";
        var default_theme = "rust";
    </script>

    <!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
        try {
            var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
            var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

            if (theme.startsWith('"') && theme.endsWith('"')) {
                localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
            }

            if (sidebar.startsWith('"') && sidebar.endsWith('"')) {
                localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
            }
        } catch (e) { }
    </script>

    <!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
        var theme;
        try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
        if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
        document.body.className = theme;
        document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
    </script>

    <!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
        var html = document.querySelector('html');
        var sidebar = 'hidden';
        if (document.body.clientWidth >= 1080) {
            try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
            sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
        }
        html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
        html.classList.add("sidebar-" + sidebar);
    </script>

        &lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
            document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
            document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
            Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
                link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
            });

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

    if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
    }
} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
    document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
    document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
    Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
        link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
    });
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
<script type="text/javascript">
var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

<body class="rust">
<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
<script type="text/javascript">
var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {

    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
<script type="text/javascript">
var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
<script type="text/javascript">
var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->

var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

var path_to_root = "";

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

&amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;

<!-- Provide site root to javascript -->
<script type="text/javascript">
var path_to_root = "";
var default_theme = "rust";
</script>


&lt;!-- Work around some values being stored in localStorage wrapped in quotes --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
    try {
        var theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme');
        var sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar');

    if (theme.startsWith('&amp;quot;') &amp;amp;&amp;amp; theme.endsWith('&amp;quot;')) {
        localStorage.setItem('mdbook-theme', theme.slice(1, theme.length - 1));
    }

if (sidebar.startsWith('&amp;amp;quot;') &amp;amp;amp;&amp;amp;amp; sidebar.endsWith('&amp;amp;quot;')) {
    localStorage.setItem('mdbook-sidebar', sidebar.slice(1, sidebar.length - 1));
}



} catch (e) { }



&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Set the theme before any content is loaded, prevents flash --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var theme;
try { theme = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-theme'); } catch(e) { }
if (theme === null || theme === undefined) { theme = default_theme; }
document.body.className = theme;
document.querySelector('html').className = theme + ' js';
&lt;/script&gt;


&lt;!-- Hide / unhide sidebar before it is displayed --&gt;
&lt;script type=&quot;text/javascript&quot;&gt;
var html = document.querySelector('html');
var sidebar = 'hidden';
if (document.body.clientWidth &gt;= 1080) {
try { sidebar = localStorage.getItem('mdbook-sidebar'); } catch(e) { }
sidebar = sidebar || 'visible';
}
html.classList.remove('sidebar-visible');
html.classList.add(&quot;sidebar-&quot; + sidebar);
&lt;/script&gt;

        &amp;amp;amp;lt;button id=&amp;amp;amp;quot;search-toggle&amp;amp;amp;quot; class=&amp;amp;amp;quot;icon-button&amp;amp;amp;quot; type=&amp;amp;amp;quot;button&amp;amp;amp;quot; title=&amp;amp;amp;quot;Search. &amp;amp;lt;!-- Apply ARIA attributes after the sidebar and the sidebar toggle button are added to the DOM --&amp;amp;gt;
&amp;amp;lt;script type=&amp;amp;quot;text/javascript&amp;amp;quot;&amp;amp;gt;
document.getElementById('sidebar-toggle').setAttribute('aria-expanded', sidebar === 'visible');
document.getElementById('sidebar').setAttribute('aria-hidden', sidebar !== 'visible');
Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#sidebar a')).forEach(function(link) {
link.setAttribute('tabIndex', sidebar === 'visible' ? 0 : -1);
});
&amp;amp;lt;/script&amp;amp;gt;
